# `calendar/Navigation`

## `Navigation Day`

####   `Day: previous button switches month to previous`

```html
<div
  aria-label="Selected none. Choose date"
  aria-live="polite"
  part="aria-selection"
>
</div>
<div part="navigation">
  <ef-button
    aria-label="Previous month"
    empty=""
    icon="left"
    part="btn-prev"
    role="button"
    tabindex="0"
    textpos="after"
  >
  </ef-button>
  <ef-button
    aria-description="Click to select year"
    icon="down"
    part="btn-view"
    role="button"
    tabindex="0"
    textpos="before"
  >
    February 2020
  </ef-button>
  <ef-button
    aria-label="Next month"
    empty=""
    icon="right"
    part="btn-next"
    role="button"
    tabindex="0"
    textpos="after"
  >
  </ef-button>
</div>
<div
  aria-multiselectable="false"
  part="table"
  role="grid"
>
  <div
    part="row day-name-row"
    role="row"
  >
    <div
```

####   `Day: next button switches month to next`

## `AD/BC Navigation Day`

####   `AD/BC Day: previous button switches month to previous`

```html
  aria-label="Selected none. Choose date"
  aria-live="polite"
  part="aria-selection"
>
</div>

  <ef-button
    aria-label="Previous month"
    empty=""
    icon="left"
    part="btn-prev"
    role="button"
    tabindex="0"
    textpos="after"
  >
  </ef-button>
  <ef-button
    aria-description="Click to select year"
    icon="down"
    part="btn-view"
    role="button"
    tabindex="0"
    textpos="before"
  >
    February 1
  </ef-button>
```

## `Navigation Month`

####   `Month: previous button switches year to previous`

```html

  aria-label="Selected none. Choose date"
  aria-live="polite"
  part="aria-selection"
>

    textpos="after"

    icon="up"
    part="btn-view"
    role="button"

    textpos="before"
```

## `AD/BC Navigation Month`

####   `AD/BC Month: previous button switches year to previous`

```html
<div
  aria-label="Selected none. Choose date"
  aria-live="polite"
  part="aria-selection"
>
</div>
<div part="navigation">
  <ef-button
    aria-label="Previous year"
    empty=""
    icon="left"
    part="btn-prev"
    role="button"
    tabindex="0"
    textpos="after"
  >
  </ef-button>
  <ef-button
    aria-description="Click to select date"
    icon="up"
    part="btn-view"
    role="button"
    tabindex="0"
    textpos="before"
  >
    1
  </ef-button>
  <ef-button
    aria-label="Next year"
    empty=""
    icon="right"
    part="btn-next"
    role="button"
    tabindex="0"
    textpos="after"
  >
  </ef-button>
```

## `Navigation Year`

####   `Year: previous button switches decade to previous`

## `AD/BC Navigation Year`

####   `AD/BC Year: previous button switches decade to previous`

```html
  aria-live="polite"
  part="aria-selection"

    aria-label="Previous decade"
    empty=""
    icon="left"
    part="btn-prev"
    role="button"
    tabindex="0"
    textpos="after"

    role="button"
```

## `View Change`

####   `View button should change views`

```html

  aria-live="polite"
  part="aria-selection"
>

  <ef-button

    empty=""

    part="btn-prev"

    tabindex="0"
    textpos="after"
  >
  </ef-button>
  <ef-button
    aria-description="Click to select year"
    icon="down"
    part="btn-view"
    role="button"
    tabindex="0"
    textpos="before"
  >
    April 2005
  </ef-button>
  <ef-button
    aria-label="Next month"

    textpos="after"
```

## `View Change Tap`

####   `View should change on tap`

```html
<div
  aria-label="Selected none. Choose date"
  aria-live="polite"
  part="aria-selection"
>
</div>
<div part="navigation">
  <ef-button
    aria-label="Previous decade"
    empty=""
    icon="left"
    part="btn-prev"
    role="button"
    tabindex="0"
    textpos="after"
  >
  </ef-button>
  <ef-button
    aria-description="Click to select date"
    icon="up"
    part="btn-view"
    role="button"
    tabindex="0"
    textpos="before"
  >
    2000 - 2015
  </ef-button>
  <ef-button
    aria-label="Next decade"

    textpos="after"
```

## `Vew Change Keyboard`

####   `Pressing escape key on month view should return to day view`

####   `Pressing escape key on year view should return to day view`

```html

  aria-label="Selected none. Choose date"
  aria-live="polite"
  part="aria-selection"
>
```
